helpers for hit testing, clickable regions, hover detection, and drag selection\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"geometry.zig\");\n+const event_mod = @import(\"event.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Position = geometry.Position;\n+pub const Mouse = event_mod.Mouse;\n+pub const MouseKind = event_mod.MouseKind;\n+\n+/// A clickable region with an identifier for hit testing.\n+/// Use this to track which UI elements receive mouse events.\n+pub fn HitRegion(comptime IdType: type) type {\n+    return struct {\n+        const Self = @This();\n+\n+        id: IdType,\n+        rect: Rect,\n+\n+        pub fn init(id: IdType, rect: Rect) Self {\n+            return .{ .id = id, .rect = rect };\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Check if a mouse event hits this region.\n+        pub fn contains(self: Self, mouse: Mouse) bool {\n+            return self.rect.contains(mouse.x, mouse.y);\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Check if a point hits this region.\n+        pub fn containsPoint(self: Self, x: u16, y: u16) bool {\n+            return self.rect.contains(x, y);\n+        }\n+    };\n+}\n+\n+/// A collection of hit regions for testing multiple areas at once.\n+/// MaxRegions is the maximum number of regions that can be registered.\n+pub fn HitTester(comptime IdType: type, comptime MaxRegions: usize) type {\n+    return struct {\n+        const Self = @This();\n+        const Region = HitRegion(IdType);\n+\n+        regions: [MaxRegions]Region = undefined,\n+        count: usize = 0,\n+\n+        pub fn init() Self {\n+            return .{};\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Register a hit region. Returns false if capacity is full.\n+        pub fn register(self: *Self, id: IdType, rect: Rect) bool {\n+            if (self.count >= MaxRegions) return false;\n+            self.regions[self.count] = Region.init(id, rect);\n+            self.count += 1;\n+            return true;\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Clear all registered regions.\n+        pub fn clear(self: *Self) void {\n+            self.count = 0;\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Find which region (if any) contains the mouse position.\n+        /// Returns the ID of the first matching region, or null if none match.\n+        /// Regions are tested in reverse order (last registered = highest priority).\n+        pub fn hitTest(self: Self, mouse: Mouse) ?IdType {\n+            return self.hitTestPoint(mouse.x, mouse.y);\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Find which region contains the given point.\n+        pub fn hitTestPoint(self: Self, x: u16, y: u16) ?IdType {\n+            // Test in reverse order for z-order priority (later = on top)\n+            var i: usize = self.count;\n+            while (i > 0) {\n+                i -= 1;\n+                if (self.regions[i].containsPoint(x, y)) {\n+                    return self.regions[i].id;\n+                }\n+            }\n+            return null;\n+        }\n+\n+        /// Get all regions that contain the mouse position.\n+        /// Useful when regions overlap and you need to know all hits.\n+        pub fn hitTestAll(self: Self, mouse: Mouse, results: []IdType) []IdType {\n+            var found: usize = 0;\n+            for (self.regions[0..self.count]) |region| {\n+                if (found >= results.len) break;\n+                if (region.contains(mouse)) {\n+                    results[found] = region.id;\n+                    found += 1;\n+                }\n+            }\n+            return results[0..found];\n+        }\n+    };\n+}\n+\n+/// Tracks hover state for a single region.\n+/// Detects enter/exit transitions.\n+pub const HoverState = struct {\n+    inside: bool = false,\n+    last_x: u16 = 0,\n+    last_y: u16 = 0,\n+\n+    /// Transition result from updating hover state.\n+    pub const Transition = enum {\n+        /// No change in hover state.\n+        none,\n+        /// Mouse entered the region.\n+        entered,\n+        /// Mouse exited the region.\n+        exited,\n+        /// Mouse moved within the region.\n+        moved,\n+    };\n+\n+    /// Update hover state with new mouse position.\n+    /// Returns the transition type.\n+    pub fn update(self: *HoverState, rect: Rect, mouse: Mouse) Transition {\n+        const now_inside = rect.contains(mouse.x, mouse.y);\n+        const was_inside = self.inside;\n+\n+        self.inside = now_inside;\n+        self.last_x = mouse.x;\n+        self.last_y = mouse.y;\n+\n+        if (now_inside and !was_inside) {\n+            return .entered;\n+        } else if (!now_inside and was_inside) {\n+            return .exited;\n+        } else if (now_inside) {\n+            return .moved;\n+        }\n+        return .none;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Reset hover state (e.g., when region moves or is hidden).\n+    pub fn reset(self: *HoverState) void {\n+        self.inside = false;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if currently hovering.\n+    pub fn isHovering(self: HoverState) bool {\n+        return self.inside;\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Tracks drag selection state.\n+/// Use for implementing click-and-drag selection of regions or text.\n+pub const DragState = struct {\n+    /// Whether a drag is currently active.\n+    active: bool = false,\n+\n+    /// Button that initiated the drag (from mouse event modifier interpretation).\n+    button_down: bool = false,\n+\n+    /// Starting position of the drag.\n+    start: Position = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 },\n+\n+    /// Current position of the drag.\n+    current: Position = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 },\n+\n+    /// Process a mouse event and update drag state.\n+    /// Returns true if a drag operation state changed.\n+    pub fn handleMouse(self: *DragState, mouse: Mouse) bool {\n+        switch (mouse.kind) {\n+            .down => {\n+                self.active = true;\n+                self.button_down = true;\n+                self.start = .{ .x = mouse.x, .y = mouse.y };\n+                self.current = self.start;\n+                return true;\n+            },\n+            .up => {\n+                if (self.active) {\n+                    self.active = false;\n+                    self.button_down = false;\n+                    self.current = .{ .x = mouse.x, .y = mouse.y };\n+                    return true;\n+                }\n+                return false;\n+            },\n+            .drag => {\n+                if (self.active) {\n+                    self.current = .{ .x = mouse.x, .y = mouse.y };\n+                    return true;\n+                }\n+                return false;\n+            },\n+            .move => {\n+                // Movement without button doesn't affect drag\n+                return false;\n+            },\n+            .scroll_up, .scroll_down => {\n+                // Scroll events don't affect drag\n+                return false;\n+            },\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Cancel the current drag operation.\n+    pub fn cancel(self: *DragState) void {\n+        self.active = false;\n+        self.button_down = false;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Reset to initial state.\n+    pub fn reset(self: *DragState) void {\n+        self.active = false;\n+        self.button_down = false;\n+        self.start = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 };\n+        self.current = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the selection rectangle (normalized so width/height are positive).\n+    /// Returns null if no drag is active.\n+    pub fn selectionRect(self: DragState) ?Rect {\n+        if (!self.active and !self.button_down) return null;\n+\n+        const x1 = @min(self.start.x, self.current.x);\n+        const y1 = @min(self.start.y, self.current.y);\n+        const x2 = @max(self.start.x, self.current.x);\n+        const y2 = @max(self.start.y, self.current.y);\n+\n+        return Rect.init(\n+            x1,\n+            y1,\n+            x2 - x1 + 1,\n+            y2 - y1 + 1,\n+        );\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if the drag has moved from its starting position.\n+    pub fn hasMoved(self: DragState) bool {\n+        return self.start.x != self.current.x or self.start.y != self.current.y;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Get the delta from start to current position.\n+    pub fn delta(self: DragState) struct { dx: i32, dy: i32 } {\n+        return .{\n+            .dx = @as(i32, self.current.x) - @as(i32, self.start.x),\n+            .dy = @as(i32, self.current.y) - @as(i32, self.start.y),\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Scroll wheel accumulator for smooth scrolling.\n+/// Accumulates scroll events and provides integer scroll amounts.\n+pub const ScrollAccumulator = struct {\n+    /// Accumulated scroll amount (can be fractional from some mice).\n+    accumulated: i32 = 0,\n+\n+    /// Number of scroll events to count as one scroll unit.\n+    /// Set higher for slower scrolling.\n+    sensitivity: i32 = 1,\n+\n+    /// Process a mouse event and return scroll delta if threshold reached.\n+    /// Returns positive for scroll down, negative for scroll up.\n+    pub fn handleMouse(self: *ScrollAccumulator, mouse: Mouse) ?i32 {\n+        switch (mouse.kind) {\n+            .scroll_up => {\n+                self.accumulated -= 1;\n+            },\n+            .scroll_down => {\n+                self.accumulated += 1;\n+            },\n+            else => return null,\n+        }\n+\n+        if (@abs(self.accumulated) >= self.sensitivity) {\n+            const result = @divTrunc(self.accumulated, self.sensitivity);\n+            self.accumulated = @rem(self.accumulated, self.sensitivity);\n+            return result;\n+        }\n+        return null;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Reset accumulated scroll.\n+    pub fn reset(self: *ScrollAccumulator) void {\n+        self.accumulated = 0;\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic type construction\n+// 16).init();\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), tester.count);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: HoverState construction\" {\n+    const hover = HoverState{};\n+    try std.testing.expect(!hover.inside);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: DragState construction\" {\n+    const drag = DragState{};\n+    try std.testing.expect(!drag.active);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: ScrollAccumulator construction\" {\n+    const scroll = ScrollAccumulator{};\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i32, 0), scroll.accumulated);\n+}\n+\n+// std.testing.expect(region.contains(Mouse.init(10, 10, .down)));\n+    try std.testing.expect(region.contains(Mouse.init(29, 29, .down)));\n+\n+    // Outside\n+    try helpers for hit testing, clickable regions, hover detection, and drag selection\n     3\n     4const std = @import(\"std\");\n     5const geometry = @import(\"geometry.zig\");\n     6const event_mod = @import(\"event.zig\");\n     7\n     8pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n     9pub const Position = geometry.Position;\n    10pub const Mouse = event_mod.Mouse;\n    11pub const MouseKind = event_mod.MouseKind;\n    12\n    13/// A clickable region with an identifier for hit testing.\n    14/// Use this to track which UI elements receive mouse events.\n    15pub fn HitRegion(comptime IdType: type) type {\n    16    return struct {\n    17        const Self = @This();\n    18\n    19        id: IdType,\n    20        rect: Rect,\n    21\n    22        pub fn init(id: IdType, rect: Rect) Self {\n    23            return .{ .id = id, .rect = rect };\n    24        }\n    25\n    26        /// Check if a mouse event hits this region.\n    27        pub fn contains(self: Self, mouse: Mouse) bool {\n    28            return self.rect.contains(mouse.x, mouse.y);\n    29        }\n    30\n    31        /// Check if a point hits this region.\n    32        pub fn containsPoint(self: Self, x: u16, y: u16) bool {\n    33            return self.rect.contains(x, y);\n    34        }\n    35    };\n    36}\n    37\n    38/// A collection of hit regions for testing multiple areas at once.\n    39/// MaxRegions is the maximum number of regions that can be registered.\n    40pub fn HitTester(comptime IdType: type, comptime MaxRegions: usize) type {\n    41    return struct {\n    42        const Self = @This();\n    43        const Region = HitRegion(IdType);\n    44\n    45        regions: [MaxRegions]Region = undefined,\n    46        count: usize = 0,\n    47\n    48        pub fn init() Self {\n    49            return .{};\n    50        }\n    51\n    52        /// Register a hit region. Returns false if capacity is full.\n    53        pub fn register(self: *Self, id: IdType, rect: Rect) bool {\n    54            if (self.count >= MaxRegions) return false;\n    55            self.regions[self.count] = Region.init(id, rect);\n    56            self.count += 1;\n    57            return true;\n    58        }\n    59\n    60        /// Clear all registered regions.\n    61        pub fn clear(self: *Self) void {\n    62            self.count = 0;\n    63        }\n    64\n    65        /// Find which region (if any) contains the mouse position.\n    66        /// Returns the ID of the first matching region, or null if none match.\n    67        /// Regions are tested in reverse order (last registered = highest priority).\n    68        pub fn hitTest(self: Self, mouse: Mouse) ?IdType {\n    69            return self.hitTestPoint(mouse.x, mouse.y);\n    70        }\n    71\n    72        /// Find which region contains the given point.\n    73        pub fn hitTestPoint(self: Self, x: u16, y: u16) ?IdType {\n    74            // Test in reverse order for z-order priority (later = on top)\n    75            var i: usize = self.count;\n    76            while (i > 0) {\n    77                i -= 1;\n    78                if (self.regions[i].containsPoint(x, y)) {\n    79                    return self.regions[i].id;\n    80                }\n    81            }\n    82            return null;\n    83        }\n    84\n    85        /// Get all regions that contain the mouse position.\n    86        /// Useful when regions overlap and you need to know all hits.\n    87        pub fn hitTestAll(self: Self, mouse: Mouse, results: []IdType) []IdType {\n    88            var found: usize = 0;\n    89            for (self.regions[0..self.count]) |region| {\n    90                if (found >= results.len) break;\n    91                if (region.contains(mouse)) {\n    92                    results[found] = region.id;\n    93                    found += 1;\n    94                }\n    95            }\n    96            return results[0..found];\n    97        }\n    98    };\n    99}\n   100\n   101/// Tracks hover state for a single region.\n   102/// Detects enter/exit transitions.\n   103pub const HoverState = struct {\n   104    inside: bool = false,\n   105    last_x: u16 = 0,\n   106    last_y: u16 = 0,\n   107\n   108    /// Transition result from updating hover state.\n   109    pub const Transition = enum {\n   110        /// No change in hover state.\n   111        none,\n   112        /// Mouse entered the region.\n   113        entered,\n   114        /// Mouse exited the region.\n   115        exited,\n   116        /// Mouse moved within the region.\n   117        moved,\n   118    };\n   119\n   120    /// Update hover state with new mouse position.\n   121    /// Returns the transition type.\n   122    pub fn update(self: *HoverState, rect: Rect, mouse: Mouse) Transition {\n   123        const now_inside = rect.contains(mouse.x, mouse.y);\n   124        const was_inside = self.inside;\n   125\n   126        self.inside = now_inside;\n   127        self.last_x = mouse.x;\n   128        self.last_y = mouse.y;\n   129\n   130        if (now_inside and !was_inside) {\n   131            return .entered;\n   132        } else if (!now_inside and was_inside) {\n   133            return .exited;\n   134        } else if (now_inside) {\n   135            return .moved;\n   136        }\n   137        return .none;\n   138    }\n   139\n   140    /// Reset hover state (e.g., when region moves or is hidden).\n   141    pub fn reset(self: *HoverState) void {\n   142        self.inside = false;\n   143    }\n   144\n   145    /// Check if currently hovering.\n   146    pub fn isHovering(self: HoverState) bool {\n   147        return self.inside;\n   148    }\n   149};\n   150\n   151/// Tracks drag selection state.\n   152/// Use for implementing click-and-drag selection of regions or text.\n   153pub const DragState = struct {\n   154    /// Whether a drag is currently active.\n   155    active: bool = false,\n   156\n   157    /// Button that initiated the drag (from mouse event modifier interpretation).\n   158    button_down: bool = false,\n   159\n   160    /// Starting position of the drag.\n   161    start: Position = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 },\n   162\n   163    /// Current position of the drag.\n   164    current: Position = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 },\n   165\n   166    /// Process a mouse event and update drag state.\n   167    /// Returns true if a drag operation state changed.\n   168    pub fn handleMouse(self: *DragState, mouse: Mouse) bool {\n   169        switch (mouse.kind) {\n   170            .down => {\n   171                self.active = true;\n   172                self.button_down = true;\n   173                self.start = .{ .x = mouse.x, .y = mouse.y };\n   174                self.current = self.start;\n   175                return true;\n   176            },\n   177            .up => {\n   178                if (self.active) {\n   179                    self.active = false;\n   180                    self.button_down = false;\n   181                    self.current = .{ .x = mouse.x, .y = mouse.y };\n   182                    return true;\n   183                }\n   184                return false;\n   185            },\n   186            .drag => {\n   187                if (self.active) {\n   188                    self.current = .{ .x = mouse.x, .y = mouse.y };\n   189                    return true;\n   190                }\n   191                return false;\n   192            },\n   193            .move => {\n   194                // Movement without button doesn't affect drag\n   195                return false;\n   196            },\n   197            .scroll_up, .scroll_down => {\n   198                // Scroll events don't affect drag\n   199                return false;\n   200            },\n   201        }\n   202    }\n   203\n   204    /// Cancel the current drag operation.\n   205    pub fn cancel(self: *DragState) void {\n   206        self.active = false;\n   207        self.button_down = false;\n   208    }\n   209\n   210    /// Reset to initial state.\n   211    pub fn reset(self: *DragState) void {\n   212        self.active = false;\n   213        self.button_down = false;\n   214        self.start = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 };\n   215        self.current = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 };\n   216    }\n   217\n   218    /// Get the selection rectangle (normalized so width/height are positive).\n   219    /// Returns null if no drag is active.\n   220    pub fn selectionRect(self: DragState) ?Rect {\n   221        if (!self.active and !self.button_down) return null;\n   222\n   223        const x1 = @min(self.start.x, self.current.x);\n   224        const y1 = @min(self.start.y, self.current.y);\n   225        const x2 = @max(self.start.x, self.current.x);\n   226        const y2 = @max(self.start.y, self.current.y);\n   227\n   228        return Rect.init(\n   229            x1,\n   230            y1,\n   231            x2 - x1 + 1,\n   232            y2 - y1 + 1,\n   233        );\n   234    }\n   235\n   236    /// Check if the drag has moved from its starting position.\n   237    pub fn hasMoved(self: DragState) bool {\n   238        return self.start.x != self.current.x or self.start.y != self.current.y;\n   239    }\n   240\n   241    /// Get the delta from start to current position.\n   242    pub fn delta(self: DragState) struct { dx: i32, dy: i32 } {\n   243        return .{\n   244            .dx = @as(i32, self.current.x) - @as(i32, self.start.x),\n   245            .dy = @as(i32, self.current.y) - @as(i32, self.start.y),\n   246        };\n   247    }\n   248};\n   249\n   250/// Scroll wheel accumulator for smooth scrolling.\n   251/// Accumulates scroll events and provides integer scroll amounts.\n   252pub const ScrollAccumulator = struct {\n   253    /// Accumulated scroll amount (can be fractional from some mice).\n   254    accumulated: i32 = 0,\n   255\n   256    /// Number of scroll events to count as one scroll unit.\n   257    /// Set higher for slower scrolling.\n   258    sensitivity: i32 = 1,\n   259\n   260    /// Process a mouse event and return scroll delta if threshold reached.\n   261    /// Returns positive for scroll down, negative for scroll up.\n   262    pub fn handleMouse(self: *ScrollAccumulator, mouse: Mouse) ?i32 {\n   263        switch (mouse.kind) {\n   264            .scroll_up => {\n   265                self.accumulated -= 1;\n   266            },\n   267            .scroll_down => {\n   268                self.accumulated += 1;\n   269            },\n   270            else => return null,\n   271        }\n   272\n   273        if (@abs(self.accumulated) >= self.sensitivity) {\n   274            const result = @divTrunc(self.accumulated, self.sensitivity);\n   275            self.accumulated = @rem(self.accumulated, self.sensitivity);\n   276            return result;\n   277        }\n   278        return null;\n   279    }\n   280\n   281    /// Reset accumulated scroll.\n   282    pub fn reset(self: *ScrollAccumulator) void {\n   283        self.accumulated = 0;\n   284    }\n   285};\n   286\n Mouse utilities for zithril TUI framework\n// Provides helpers for hit testing, clickable regions, hover detection, and drag selection\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst geometry = @import(\"geometry.zig\");\nconst event_mod = @import(\"event.zig\");\n\npub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\npub const Position = geometry.Position;\npub const Mouse = event_mod.Mouse;\npub const MouseKind = event_mod.MouseKind;\n\n/// A clickable region with an identifier for hit testing.\n/// Use this to track which UI elements receive mouse events.\npub fn HitRegion(comptime IdType: type) type {\n    return struct {\n        const Self = @This();\n\n        id: IdType,\n        rect: Rect,\n\n        pub fn init(id: IdType, rect: Rect) Self {\n            return .{ .id = id, .rect = rect };\n        }\n\n        /// Check if a mouse event hits this region.\n        pub fn contains(self: Self, mouse: Mouse) bool {\n            return self.rect.contains(mouse.x, mouse.y);\n        }\n\n        /// Check if a point hits this region.\n        pub fn containsPoint(self: Self, x: u16, y: u16) bool {\n            return self.rect.contains(x, y);\n        }\n    };\n}\n\n/// A collection of hit regions for testing multiple areas at once.\n/// MaxRegions is the maximum number of regions that can be registered.\npub fn HitTester(comptime IdType: type, comptime MaxRegions: usize) type {\n    return struct {\n        const Self = @This();\n        const Region = HitRegion(IdType);\n\n        regions: [MaxRegions]Region = undefined,\n        count: usize = 0,\n\n        pub fn init() Self {\n            return .{};\n        }\n\n        /// Register a hit region. Returns false if capacity is full.\n        pub fn register(self: *Self, id: IdType, rect: Rect) bool {\n            if (self.count >= MaxRegions) return false;\n            self.regions[self.count] = Region.init(id, rect);\n            self.count += 1;\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        /// Clear all registered regions.\n        pub fn clear(self: *Self) void {\n            self.count = 0;\n        }\n\n        /// Find which region (if any) contains the mouse position.\n        /// Returns the ID of the first matching region, or null if none match.\n        /// Regions are tested in reverse order (last registered = highest priority).\n        pub fn hitTest(self: Self, mouse: Mouse) ?IdType {\n            return self.hitTestPoint(mouse.x, mouse.y);\n        }\n\n        /// Find which region contains the given point.\n        pub fn hitTestPoint(self: Self, x: u16, y: u16) ?IdType {\n            // Test in reverse order for z-order priority (later = on top)\n            var i: usize = self.count;\n            while (i > 0) {\n                i -= 1;\n                if (self.regions[i].containsPoint(x, y)) {\n                    return self.regions[i].id;\n                }\n            }\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        /// Get all regions that contain the mouse position.\n        /// Useful when regions overlap and you need to know all hits.\n        pub fn hitTestAll(self: Self, mouse: Mouse, results: []IdType) []IdType {\n            var found: usize = 0;\n            for (self.regions[0..self.count]) |region| {\n                if (found >= results.len) break;\n                if (region.contains(mouse)) {\n                    results[found] = region.id;\n                    found += 1;\n                }\n            }\n            return results[0..found];\n        }\n    };\n}\n\n/// Tracks hover state for a single region.\n/// Detects enter/exit transitions.\npub const HoverState = struct {\n    inside: bool = false,\n    last_x: u16 = 0,\n    last_y: u16 = 0,\n\n    /// Transition result from updating hover state.\n    pub const Transition = enum {\n        /// No change in hover state.\n        none,\n        /// Mouse entered the region.\n        entered,\n        /// Mouse exited the region.\n        exited,\n        /// Mouse moved within the region.\n        moved,\n    };\n\n    /// Update hover state with new mouse position.\n    /// Returns the transition type.\n    pub fn update(self: *HoverState, rect: Rect, mouse: Mouse) Transition {\n        const now_inside = rect.contains(mouse.x, mouse.y);\n        const was_inside = self.inside;\n\n        self.inside = now_inside;\n        self.last_x = mouse.x;\n        self.last_y = mouse.y;\n\n        if (now_inside and !was_inside) {\n            return .entered;\n        } else if (!now_inside and was_inside) {\n            return .exited;\n        } else if (now_inside) {\n            return .moved;\n        }\n        return .none;\n    }\n\n    /// Reset hover state (e.g., when region moves or is hidden).\n    pub fn reset(self: *HoverState) void {\n        self.inside = false;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if currently hovering.\n    pub fn isHovering(self: HoverState) bool {\n        return self.inside;\n    }\n};\n\n/// Tracks drag selection state.\n/// Use for implementing click-and-drag selection of regions or text.\npub const DragState = struct {\n    /// Whether a drag is currently active.\n    active: bool = false,\n\n    /// Button that initiated the drag (from mouse event modifier interpretation).\n    button_down: bool = false,\n\n    /// Starting position of the drag.\n    start: Position = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 },\n\n    /// Current position of the drag.\n    current: Position = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 },\n\n    /// Process a mouse event and update drag state.\n    /// Returns true if a drag operation state changed.\n    pub fn handleMouse(self: *DragState, mouse: Mouse) bool {\n        switch (mouse.kind) {\n            .down => {\n                self.active = true;\n                self.button_down = true;\n                self.start = .{ .x = mouse.x, .y = mouse.y };\n                self.current = self.start;\n                return true;\n            },\n            .up => {\n                if (self.active) {\n                    self.active = false;\n                    self.button_down = false;\n                    self.current = .{ .x = mouse.x, .y = mouse.y };\n                    return true;\n                }\n                return false;\n            },\n            .drag => {\n                if (self.active) {\n                    self.current = .{ .x = mouse.x, .y = mouse.y };\n                    return true;\n                }\n                return false;\n            },\n            .move => {\n                // Movement without button doesn't affect drag\n                return false;\n            },\n            .scroll_up, .scroll_down => {\n                // Scroll events don't affect drag\n                return false;\n            },\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Cancel the current drag operation.\n    pub fn cancel(self: *DragState) void {\n        self.active = false;\n        self.button_down = false;\n    }\n\n    /// Reset to initial state.\n    pub fn reset(self: *DragState) void {\n        self.active = false;\n        self.button_down = false;\n        self.start = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 };\n        self.current = .{ .x = 0, .y = 0 };\n    }\n\n    /// Get the selection rectangle (normalized so width/height are positive).\n    /// Returns null if no drag is active.\n    pub fn selectionRect(self: DragState) ?Rect {\n        if (!self.active and !self.button_down) return null;\n\n        const x1 = @min(self.start.x, self.current.x);\n        const y1 = @min(self.start.y, self.current.y);\n        const x2 = @max(self.start.x, self.current.x);\n        const y2 = @max(self.start.y, self.current.y);\n\n        return Rect.init(\n            x1,\n            y1,\n            x2 - x1 + 1,\n            y2 - y1 + 1,\n        );\n    }\n\n    /// Check if the drag has moved from its starting position.\n    pub fn hasMoved(self: DragState) bool {\n        return self.start.x != self.current.x or self.start.y != self.current.y;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the delta from start to current position.\n    pub fn delta(self: DragState) struct { dx: i32, dy: i32 } {\n        return .{\n            .dx = @as(i32, self.current.x) - @as(i32, self.start.x),\n            .dy = @as(i32, self.current.y) - @as(i32, self.start.y),\n        };\n    }\n};\n\n/// Scroll wheel accumulator for smooth scrolling.\n/// Accumulates scroll events and provides integer scroll amounts.\npub const ScrollAccumulator = struct {\n    /// Accumulated scroll amount (can be fractional from some mice).\n    accumulated: i32 = 0,\n\n    /// Number of scroll events to count as one scroll unit.\n    /// Set higher for slower scrolling.\n    sensitivity: i32 = 1,\n\n    /// Process a mouse event and return scroll delta if threshold reached.\n    /// Returns positive for scroll down, negative for scroll up.\n    pub fn handleMouse(self: *ScrollAccumulator, mouse: Mouse) ?i32 {\n        switch (mouse.kind) {\n            .scroll_up => {\n                self.accumulated -= 1;\n            },\n            .scroll_down => {\n                self.accumulated += 1;\n            },\n            else => return null,\n        }\n\n        if (@abs(self.accumulated) >= self.sensitivity) {\n            const result = @divTrunc(self.accumulated, self.sensitivity);\n            self.accumulated = @rem(self.accumulated, self.sensitivity);\n            return result;\n        }\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Reset accumulated scroll.\n    pub fn reset(self: *ScrollAccumulator) void {\n        self.accumulated = 0;\n    }\n};\n\n// offline,\n\n    fn symbol(self: AgentStatus) []const u8 {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .idle => \"[*]\",\n            .running => \"[>]\",\n            .failed => \"[!]\",\n            .offline => \"[-]\",\n        };\n    }\n\n    fn color(self: AgentStatus) zithril.Color {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .idle => .green,\n            .running => .cyan,\n            .failed => .red,\n            .offline => .white,\n        };\n    }\n};\n\n// Agent data\nconst Agent = struct {\n    name: []const u8,\n    status: AgentStatus,\n    tasks_completed: u32,\n    tasks_total: u32,\n    last_activity: []const u8,\n};\n\n// Log entry\nconst LogEntry = struct {\n    timestamp: []const u8,\n    level: LogLevel,\n    message: []const u8,\n};\n\nconst LogLevel = enum {\n    info,\n    warning,\n    err,\n    debug,\n\n    fn prefix(self: LogLevel) []const u8 {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .info => \"[INFO]\",\n            .warning => \"[WARN]\",\n            .err => \"[ERR ]\",\n            .debug => \"[DBG ]\",\n        };\n    }\n\n    fn color(self: LogLevel) zithril.Color {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .info => .cyan,\n            .warning => .yellow,\n            .err => .red,\n            .debug => .white,\n        };\n    }\n};\n\n// Application state\nconst State = struct {\n    focus: Focus = .agents,\n    selected_agent: usize = 0,\n    log_scroll: usize = 0,\n    agents: []const Agent,\n    logs: []const LogEntry,\n\n    fn selectNextAgent(self: *State) void {\n        if (self.agents.len == 0) return;\n        if (self.selected_agent < self.agents.len - 1) {\n            self.selected_agent += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn selectPrevAgent(self: *State) void {\n        if (self.selected_agent > 0) {\n            self.selected_agent -= 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn scrollLogsDown(self: *State) void {\n        if (self.logs.len > 0) {\n            self.log_scroll +|= 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn scrollLogsUp(self: *State) void {\n        if (self.log_scroll > 0) {\n            self.log_scroll -= 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn cycleFocus(self: *State) void {\n        self.focus = switch (self.focus) {\n            .agents => .logs,\n            .logs => .agents,\n        };\n    }\n\n    fn getSelectedAgent(self: *State) ?*const Agent {\n        if (self.agents.len == 0) return null;\n        const idx = @min(self.selected_agent, self.agents.len - 1);\n        return &self.agents[idx];\n    }\n};\n\n// Handle events\nfn update(state: *State, event: zithril.Event) zithril.Action {\n    switch (event) {\n        .key => |key| {\n            if (!key.modifiers.any()) {\n                switch (key.code) {\n                    .char => |c| switch (c) {\n                        'q' => return .quit,\n                        'j' => handleDown(state),\n                        'k' => handleUp(state),\n                        else => {},\n                    },\n                    .up => handleUp(state),\n                    .down => handleDown(state),\n                    .tab => state.cycleFocus(),\n                    else => {},\n                }\n            } else if (key.modifiers.shift) {\n                switch (key.code) {\n                    .backtab => state.cycleFocus(),\n                    else => {},\n                }\n            }\n        },\n        else => {},\n    }\n    return .none;\n}\n\nfn handleDown(state: *State) void {\n    switch (state.focus) {\n        .agents => state.selectNextAgent(),\n        .logs => state.scrollLogsDown(),\n    }\n}\n\nfn handleUp(state: *State) void {\n    switch (state.focus) {\n        .agents => state.selectPrevAgent(),\n        .logs => state.scrollLogsUp(),\n    }\n}\n\n// Render the UI\nfn view(state: *State, frame: *zithril.Frame(zithril.App(State).DefaultMaxWidgets)) void {\n    const area = frame.size();\n\n    // Main layout: status bar at bottom\n    const main_chunks = zithril.layout(area, .vertical, &.{\n        zithril.Constraint.flexible(1),\n        zithril.Constraint.len(1),\n    });\n\n    renderMainContent(state, frame, main_chunks.get(0));\n    renderStatusBar(state, frame, main_chunks.get(1));\n}\n\nfn renderMainContent(state: *State, frame: *zithril.Frame(zithril.App(State).DefaultMaxWidgets), area: zithril.Rect) void {\n    // Split into left (agents) and right (detail + logs)\n    const h_chunks = zithril.layout(area, .horizontal, &.{\n        zithril.Constraint.len(30),\n        zithril.Constraint.flexible(1),\n    });\n\n    renderAgentList(state, frame, h_chunks.get(0));\n    renderRightPanel(state, frame, h_chunks.get(1));\n}\n\nfn renderAgentList(state: *State, frame: *zithril.Frame(zithril.App(State).DefaultMaxWidgets), area: zithril.Rect) void {\n    const is_focused = state.focus == .agents;\n    const border_color: zithril.Color = if (is_focused) .cyan else .white;\n\n    const block = zithril.Block{\n        .title = if (is_focused) \"Agents [*]\" else \"Agents\",\n        .border = .rounded,\n        .border_style = zithril.Style.init().fg(border_color),\n    };\n    frame.render(block, area);\n\n    const inner = block.inner(area);\n    if (inner.isEmpty()) return;\n\n    // Build agent display strings\n    var items: [16][]const u8 = undefined;\n    var bufs: [16][64]u8 = undefined;\n    const count = @min(state.agents.len, 16);\n\n    for (state.agents[0..count], 0..count) |agent, i| {\n        const display = std.fmt.bufPrint(&bufs[i], \"{s} {s}\", .{ agent.status.symbol(), agent.name }) catch agent.name;\n        items[i] = display;\n    }\n\n    const list = zithril.List{\n        .items = items[0..count],\n        .selected = if (is_focused) state.selected_agent else null,\n        .style = zithril.Style.init().fg(.white),\n        .highlight_style = zithril.Style.init().bg(.blue).fg(.white).bold(),\n        .highlight_symbol = \"> \",\n    };\n    frame.render(list, inner);\n}\n\nfn renderRightPanel(state: *State, frame: *zithril.Frame(zithril.App(State).DefaultMaxWidgets), area: zithril.Rect) void {\n    // Split into detail (top) and logs (bottom)\n    const v_chunks = zithril.layout(area, .vertical, &.{\n        zithril.Constraint.len(10),\n        zithril.Constraint.flexible(1),\n    });\n\n    renderAgentDetail(state, frame, v_chunks.get(0));\n    renderLogPanel(state, frame, v_chunks.get(1));\n}\n\nfn renderAgentDetail(state: *State, frame: *zithril.Frame(zithril.App(State).DefaultMaxWidgets), area: zithril.Rect) void {\n    const block = zithril.Block{\n        .title = \"Agent Details\",\n        .border = .rounded,\n        .border_style = zithril.Style.init().fg(.white),\n    };\n    frame.render(block, area);\n\n    const inner = block.inner(area);\n    if (inner.isEmpty()) return;\n\n    if (state.getSelectedAgent()) |agent| {\n        // Split inner area for details and gauge\n        const detail_chunks = zithril.layout(inner, .vertical, &.{\n            zithril.Constraint.flexible(1),\n            zithril.Constraint.len(1),\n        });\n\n        // Agent info\n        var buf: [256]u8 = undefined;\n        const info_text = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf,\n            \\\\Name: {s}\n            \\\\Status: {s}\n            \\\\Last Activity: {s}\n            \\\\Tasks: {d}/{d}\n        , .{\n            agent.name,\n            @tagName(agent.status),\n            agent.last_activity,\n            agent.tasks_completed,\n            agent.tasks_total,\n        }) catch \"No data\";\n\n        const para = zithril.Paragraph{\n            .text = info_text,\n            .style = zithril.Style.init().fg(.white),\n            .wrap = .none,\n        };\n        frame.render(para, detail_chunks.get(0));\n\n        // Progress gauge\n        const ratio: f32 = if (agent.tasks_total > 0)\n            @as(f32, @floatFromInt(agent.tasks_completed)) / @as(f32, @floatFromInt(agent.tasks_total))\n        else\n            0.0;\n\n        var gauge_label_buf: [16]u8 = undefined;\n        const gauge_label = std.fmt.bufPrint(&gauge_label_buf, \"{d}%\", .{@as(u8, @intFromFloat(ratio * 100))}) catch \"\";\n\n        const gauge = zithril.Gauge{\n            .ratio = ratio,\n            .label = gauge_label,\n            .style = zithril.Style.init().bg(.black),\n            .gauge_style = zithril.Style.init().bg(agent.status.color()),\n        };\n        frame.render(gauge, detail_chunks.get(1));\n    } else {\n        const text = zithril.Text{\n            .content = \"No agent selected\",\n            .style = zithril.Style.init().fg(.white).italic(),\n            .alignment = .center,\n        };\n        frame.render(text, inner);\n    }\n}\n\nfn renderLogPanel(state: *State, frame: *zithril.Frame(zithril.App(State).DefaultMaxWidgets), area: zithril.Rect) void {\n    const is_focused = state.focus == .logs;\n    const border_color: zithril.Color = if (is_focused) .cyan else .white;\n\n    const block = zithril.Block{\n        .title = if (is_focused) \"Logs [*]\" else \"Logs\",\n        .border = .rounded,\n        .border_style = zithril.Style.init().fg(border_color),\n    };\n    frame.render(block, area);\n\n    const inner = block.inner(area);\n    if (inner.isEmpty()) return;\n\n    // Calculate visible log range\n    const visible_lines = inner.height;\n    const max_scroll = if (state.logs.len > visible_lines)\n        state.logs.len - visible_lines\n    else\n        0;\n    const scroll_offset = @min(state.log_scroll, max_scroll);\n\n    // Render visible logs\n    var y: u16 = 0;\n    const end_idx = @min(scroll_offset + visible_lines, state.logs.len);\n\n    for (state.logs[scroll_offset..end_idx]) |entry| {\n        if (y >= inner.height) break;\n\n        // Format log line\n        var line_buf: [128]u8 = undefined;\n        const line = std.fmt.bufPrint(&line_buf, \"{s} {s} {s}\", .{\n            entry.timestamp,\n            entry.level.prefix(),\n            entry.message,\n        }) catch entry.message;\n\n        const text = zithril.Text{\n            .content = line,\n            .style = zithril.Style.init().fg(entry.level.color()),\n            .alignment = .left,\n        };\n\n        const line_area = visible_lines) {\n        const scrollbar_area = zithril.Rect.init(area.right() -| 1, inner.y, 1, inner.height);\n        const scrollbar = zithril.Scrollbar{\n            .total = state.logs.len,\n            .position = scroll_offset,\n            .viewport = visible_lines,\n            .style = zithril.Style.init().fg(.white),\n            .orientation = .vertical,\n        };\n        frame.render(scrollbar, scrollbar_area);\n    }\n}\n\nfn renderStatusBar(state: *State, frame: *zithril.Frame(zithril.App(State).DefaultMaxWidgets), area: zithril.Rect) void {\n    _ = state;\n\n \"Ralph | Connected | q:Quit Tab:Focus j/k:Navigate\";\n    const text = zithril.Text{\n        .content = status_text,\n        .style = zithril.Style.init().fg(.white).bg(.blue).bold(),\n        .alignment = .left,\n    };\n    frame.render(text, area);\n}\n\n// Sample data\nconst sample_agents = [_]Agent{\n    .{ .name = \"agent-alpha\", .status = .running, .tasks_completed = 42, .tasks_total = 100, .last_activity = \"2m ago\" },\n    .{ .name = \"agent-beta\", .status = .idle, .tasks_completed = 100, .tasks_total = 100, .last_activity = \"5m ago\" },\n    .{ .name = \"agent-gamma\", .status = .failed, .tasks_completed = 23, .tasks_total = 50, .last_activity = \"1m ago\" },\n    .{ .name = \"agent-delta\", .status = .running, .tasks_completed = 78, .tasks_total = 200, .last_activity = \"30s ago\" },\n    .{ .name = \"agent-epsilon\", .status = .offline, .tasks_completed = 0, .tasks_total = 0, .last_activity = \"1h ago\" },\n    .{ .name = \"agent-zeta\",       return .{\n   101                .alternate_screen = self.alternate_screen,\n   102                .hide_cursor = true,\n   103                .mouse_capture = self.mouse_capture,\n   104                .bracketed_paste = self.paste_bracket,\n   105            };\n   106        }\n   107\n   108        /// Call the update function with an event.\n   109        /// Returns the action to be OutOfMemory,\n   123            NotATty,\n   124            TerminalQueryFailed,\n   125            TerminalSetFailed,\n   126            IoError,\n   127        };\n   128\n   129        /// Run the Poll for events (keyboard, mouse, resize, or tick timeout)\n   133        /// 2. Call update function with the event\n   134        /// 3. Check action - if .quit, exit loop\n   135        /// 4. Call view function to describe the UI\n   136        /// 5. Render by diffing buffers and writing changes to terminal\n   137        /// 6. Repeat\n   138        pub fn run(self: *Self, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) RunError!void {\n   139            // Initialize terminal backend\n   140            var backend =           };\n   165            defer previous_buf.deinit();\n   166\n   167            // Allocate update buffer for diff results\n   168            const max_updates = @as(usize, initial_size.width) * @as(usize, initial_size.height);\n   169            var updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, max_updates) catch {\n   170                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n   171            };\n   172            defer allocator.free(updates);\n   173\n   174            // Calculate tick timeout in nanoseconds (0 means no timeout/poll mode)\n   175            const tick_timeout_ns: ?u64 = if (self.tick_rate_ms > 0)\n   176                @as(u64, self.tick_rate_ms) * std.time.ns_per_ms\n   177            else\n   178                null;\n   179\n   180            // Track last tick time for tick events\n   181            var last_tick: i128 = std.time.nanoTimestamp();\n   182\n   183            // Clear screen initially\n   184            backend.clearScreen();\n   185 Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets).init(&current_buf);\n   191                self.view(&frame);\n   192                try renderBuffer(&backend, &current_buf, &previous_buf, updates);\n   193                @memcpy(previous_buf.cells, current_buf.cells);\n   194            }\n   195\n   196            // Main event loop\n   197            while (true) {\n   198                // Poll for events or wait for tick timeout\n   199                const maybe_event = try pollEvent(&input, &backend, tick_timeout_ns);\n   200\n   201                // Handle tick event generation\n   202                const event: Event = if (maybe_event) |e|\n   203                    e\n   204                else if (tick_timeout_ns) |timeout| blk: {\n   205                    const now = std.time.nanoTimestamp();\n   206                    if (now - last_tick >= @as(i128, timeout)) {\n   207                        last_tick = now;\n   208                        break :blk Event{ .tick = {} };\n   209                    }\n   210                    continue;\n   211                } else continue;\n   212\n   213                // Handle resize events specially - resize buffers\n   214                if (event == .resize) {\n   215                    const new_size = event.resize;\n   216                    const new_max_updates = @as(usize, new_size.width) * @as(usize, new_size.height);\n   217\n   218                    current_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n   219                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n   220                    };\n   221                    previous_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n   222                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n   223                    };\n   224\n   225                    allocator.free(updates);\n   226                    updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, new_max_updates) catch {\n   227                        return (*State, Event) Action,\n            /// View function pointer.\n            view: *const fn (*State, *Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets)) void,\n            /// Timer interval in milliseconds for tick events paste_bracket: bool = false,\n            /// Use alternate screen buffer.\n            alternate_screen: bool = true,\n        };\n\n        /// Initialize an App with the given configuration.\n   .tick_rate_ms = config.tick_rate_ms,\n                .mouse_capture = config.mouse_capture,\n                .paste_bracket = config.paste_bracket,\n                .alternate_screen = config.alternate_screen,\n            };\n        }\n\n        /// Returns a BackendConfig derived from this App's configuration.\n        /// Used by the event loop to initialize the terminal backend.\n        pub fn backendConfig(self: Self) @import(\"backend.zig\").BackendConfig {\n            return .{\n                .alternate_screen = self.alternate_screen,\n                .hide_cursor = true,\n                .mouse_capture = self.mouse_capture,\n                .bracketed_paste = self.paste_bracket,\n            };\n        }\n\n        /// Call the update function with an event.\n        /// Returns the action to be processed by the runtime.\n        pub fn update(self: *Self, event: Event) Action {\n            return self.update_fn(&self.state, event);\n        }\n\n        /// Call the view function with a frame.\n        /// The view function should use frame.render() to draw widgets.\n        pub fn view(self: *Self, frame: *Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets)) void {\n            self.view_fn(&self.state, frame);\n        }\n\n        /// Error type for run operations.\n        pub const RunError = error{\n            OutOfMemory,\n            NotATty,\n            TerminalQueryFailed,\n            TerminalSetFailed,\n            IoError,\n        };\n\n        /// Run the main event loop until Action.quit is returned.\n        ///\n        /// Main loop:\n        /// 1. Poll for events (keyboard, mouse, resize, or tick timeout)\n        /// 2. Call update function with the event\n        /// 3. Check action - if .quit, exit loop\n        /// 4. Call view function to describe the UI\n        /// 5. Render by diffing buffers and writing changes to terminal\n        /// 6. Repeat\n        pub fn run(self: *Self, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) RunError!void {\n            // Initialize terminal backend\n            var backend = Backend.init(self.backendConfig()) catch |err| {\n                return switch (err) {\n                    error.NotATty => RunError.NotATty,\n                    error.TerminalQueryFailed => RunError.TerminalQueryFailed,\n                    error.TerminalSetFailed => RunError.TerminalSetFailed,\n                    error.IoError => RunError.IoError,\n                };\n            };\n            defer backend.deinit();\n\n            // Initialize input parser\n            var input = Input.init();\n\n            // Get initial terminal size\n            const initial_size = backend.getSize();\n\n            // Create double buffers for diffing\n            var current_buf = Buffer.init(allocator, initial_size.width, initial_size.height) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer current_buf.deinit();\n\n            var previous_buf = Buffer.init(allocator, initial_size.width, initial_size.height) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer previous_buf.deinit();\n\n            // Allocate update buffer for diff results\n            const max_updates = @as(usize, initial_size.width) * @as(usize, initial_size.height);\n            var updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, max_updates) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer allocator.free(updates);\n\n            // Calculate tick timeout in nanoseconds (0 means no timeout/poll mode)\n            const tick_timeout_ns: ?u64 = if (self.tick_rate_ms > 0)\n                @as(u64, self.tick_rate_ms) * std.time.ns_per_ms\n            else\n                null;\n\n            // Track last tick time for tick events\n            var last_tick: i128 = std.time.nanoTimestamp();\n\n            // Clear screen initially\n            backend.clearScreen();\n            backend.cursorHome();\n\n            // Initial render\n            {\n                current_buf.clear();\n                var frame = Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets).init(&current_buf);\n                self.view(&frame);\n                try renderBuffer(&backend, &current_buf, &previous_buf, updates);\n                @memcpy(previous_buf.cells, current_buf.cells);\n            }\n\n            // Main event loop\n            while (true) {\n                // Poll for events or wait for tick timeout\n              last_tick = now;\n                        break :blk Event{ .tick = {} };\n                    }\n                    continue;\n                } else continue;\n\n                // Handle resize events specially - resize buffers\n                if (event == .resize) {\n                    const new_size = event.resize;\n                    const new_max_updates = @as(usize, new_size.width) * @as(usize, new_size.height);\n\n                    current_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n                    previous_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n\n                    allocator.free(updates);\n                    updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, new_max_updates) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n\n                    // Clear screen on resize\n                    backend.clearScreen();\n                    backend.cursorHome();\n                }\n\n                // Call update function\n                const action = self.update(event);\n\n                // Check for quit action\n                if (action.isQuit()) {\n                    break;\n                }\n\n &previous_buf, updates);\n\n                // Swap buffers (copy current to previous for next diff)\n                @memcpy(previous_buf.cells, current_buf.cells);\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// Poll for an input event from the terminal.\n        /// Returns null if no event is available within the timeout.\n        fn pollEvent(input: *Input, backend: *Backend, timeout_ns: ?u64) RunError!?Event {\n            _ = timeout_ns; // TODO: Implement proper polling with timeout\n\n            // Read available input bytes\n            var buf: [256]u8 = undefined;\n            const bytes_read = std.posix.read(std.posix.STDIN_FILENO, &buf) catch |err| {\n                switch (err) {\n                    error.WouldBlock => return null,\n                    else => return RunError.IoError,\n                }\n            };\n\n            if (bytes_read == 0) {\n                return null;\n            }\n\n            // Parse input bytes into events\n            if (input.parse(buf[0..bytes_read])) |parsed_event| {\n                _ = backend; // Backend used for future resize detection\n                return parsed_event;\n            }\n\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        /// Render buffer changes to the terminal using buffered Output.\n        /// Uses rich_zig's ANSI rendering for proper color and attribute output.\n        fn renderBuffer(\n            backend: *Backend,\n            current: *Buffer,\n            previous: *Buffer,\n            update_buffer: []buffer_mod.CellUpdate,\n        ) RunError!void {\n            const changes = current.diff(previous.*, update_buffer);\n\n            if (changes.len == 0) {\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // Use buffered output with rich_zig ANSI rendering\n            var out = backend_mod.DefaultOutput.init(backend.handle);\n\n            var last_x: ?u16 = null;\n            var last_y: ?u16 = null;\n\n            for (changes) |change| {\n                // Move cursor if not consecutive (different row or non-adjacent column)\n                const consecutive = last_x != null and last_y != null and\n                    last_y.? == change.y and last_x.? + 1 == change.x;\n\n                if (!consecutive) {\n                    out.cursorTo(change.x, change.y);\n                }\n\n                // Set style using rich_zig ANSI rendering\n                if (!change.cell.style.isEmpty()) {\n                    out.setStyle(change.cell.style);\n                } else {\n                    out.resetStyle();\n                }\n\n                // Write character\n                if (change.cell.width > 0) {\n                    out.writeChar(change.cell.char, backend_mod.Style.empty);\n                }\n\n                last_x = change.x;\n                last_y = change.y;\n            }\n\n            // Reset style at the end\n            out.resetStyle();\n\n            // Flush buffered output to terminal\n            out.flush();\n        }\n    };\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic App construction\n// *SimpleState, event: Event) Action {\n        _ = event;\n        state.count += 1;\n        return Action.none_action;\n    }\n\n    fn simpleView(state: *SimpleState, frame: *Frame(App(SimpleState).DefaultMaxWidgets)) void {\n        _ = state;\n        _ = frame;\n    }\n\n    const EmptyState = struct {};\n\n    fn emptyUpdate(state: *EmptyState, event: Event) Action {\n        _ = state;\n        _ = event;\n        return Action.none_action;\n    }\n\n    fn emptyView(state: *EmptyState, frame: *Frame(App(EmptyState).DefaultMaxWidgets)) void {\n        _ = state;\n        _ = frame;\n    }\n\n    fn quitOnEscapeUpdate(state: *EmptyState, event: Event) Action {\n        _ = state;\n        switch (event) {\n            .key => |key| {\n                if (key.code == .escape) {\n                    return Action.quit_action;\n                }\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n        return Action.none_action;\n    }\n};\n\ntest \"sanity: App init with simple state\" {\n    const app = App(TestHelpers.SimpleState).init(.{\n        .state = .{ .count = 42 },\n        .update = TestHelpers.simpleUpdate,\n        .view = TestHelpers.simpleView,\n    });\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i32, 42), app.state.count);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: App update modifies state\" {\n    var app = App(TestHelpers.SimpleState).init(.{\n        .state = .{ .count = 0 },\n        .update = TestHelpers.simpleUpdate,\n        .view = TestHelpers.simpleView,\n    });\n\n    _ = app.update(Event{ .tick = {} });\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i32, 1), app.state.count);\n\n    _ = app.update(Event{ .tick = {} });\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(i32, 2), app.state.count);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: App update returns quit action\" {\n    var app = App(TestHelpers.EmptyState).init(.{\n        .state = .{},\n        .update = TestHelpers.quitOnEscapeUpdate,\n        .view = TestHelpers.emptyView,\n    });\n\n    const action1 = app.update(Event{ .tick = {} });\n    try std.testing.expect(action1.isNone());\n\n    const action2 = app.update(Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } });\n    try std.testing.expect(action2.isQuit());\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - App with complex state\n// inner: Inner,\n        name: []const u8,\n    };\n\n    fn nestedUpdate(state: *NestedState, event: Event) Action {\n        _ = event;\n        state.inner.value += 1;\n        return Action.none_action;\n    }\n\n    fn nestedView(state: *NestedState, frame: *Frame(App(NestedState).DefaultMaxWidgets)) void {\n        _ = state;\n        _ = frame;\n    }\n};\n\ntest \"behavior: App with nested state\" {\n    var app = App(NestedTestHelpers.NestedState).init(.{\n        .state = .{\n            .inner = .{ .value = 100 },\n            .name = \"test\",\n        },\n .tick = {} });\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u32, 101), app.state.inner.value);\n}\n\nconst ViewTestHelpers = struct {\n    const RenderState = struct {\n        rendered: bool = false,\n Event) Action {\n        state.last_event_type = switch (event) {\n            .key => .key,\n            .mouse => .mouse,\n            .resize => .resize,\n            .tick => .tick,\n            .command_result => .command_result,\n        };\n        return Action.none_action;\n    }\n\n    fn trackingView(state: *TrackingState, frame: *Frame(App(TrackingState).DefaultMaxWidgets)) void {\n        _ = state;\n        _ = frame;\n    }\n};\n\ntest \"regression: App handles all event types in update\" {\n    var app = App(EventTrackingHelpers.TrackingState).init(.{\n        .state = .{},\n
